\DoxyCodeLine{02321\ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{case}\ WM\_SETFOCUS:}
\DoxyCodeLine{02322\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ You\ would\ think\ that\ this\ would\ be\ a\ good\ time\ to\ call}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02323\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ resend\_lost\_keypresses(),\ but\ it\ turns\ out\ that\ we\ get\ WM\_SETFOCUS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02324\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ slightly\ before\ Windows\ starts\ resending\ key\ updown\ events\ to\ us.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02325\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02326\ \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02327\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ In\ particular,\ if\ the\ user\ restored\ focus\ using\ alt-\/tab,\ then\ at\ this\ point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02328\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ the\ keyboard\ state\ will\ indicate\ that\ both\ the\ alt\ and\ tab\ keys\ are\ held}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02329\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ down.\ \ However,\ there\ is\ a\ small\ window\ of\ opportunity\ for\ the\ user\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02330\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ release\ these\ keys\ before\ Windows\ starts\ telling\ us\ about\ keyup\ events.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02331\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ Thus,\ if\ we\ record\ the\ fact\ that\ alt\ and\ tab\ are\ being\ held\ down\ now,\ we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02332\ \textcolor{comment}{\ *\ may\ miss\ the\ keyup\ events\ for\ them,\ and\ they\ can\ get\ "{}stuck"{}\ down.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02333\ \textcolor{comment}{\ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02334\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02335\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ So\ we\ have\ to\ defer\ calling\ resend\_lost\_keypresses()\ until\ we\ know}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02336\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Windows\ is\ ready\ to\ send\ us\ key\ updown\ events.\ \ I\ don't\ know\ when\ we}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02337\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ can\ guarantee\ that,\ except\ when\ we\ actually\ do\ start\ to\ receive\ key}}
\DoxyCodeLine{02338\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ updown\ events,\ so\ that\ call\ is\ made\ there.}}
